**Evaluation:**    **Output (a)** and **Output (b)** present different definitions of collusion.    **Output (a)** emphasizes the active act of conspiring or collaborating in wrongdoing. It defines collusion as ranging from the failure to keep records and withholding intelligence to agents being involved in murder. This definition is broad and includes both positive and negative acts.    **Output (b)** focuses more on the omission or failure to act.
